<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Interim
Management Report</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">1. Business
Activity</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON (&#147;the AIXTRON Group&#148; or &#147;the Company&#148;) is a
leading provider of deposition equipment to the semiconductor industry. The
Company&#146;s technology solutions are used by a diverse range of customers
worldwide to build advanced components for electronic and opto-electronic
applications based on compound, silicon, or organic semiconductor materials.
Such components are used in displays, signaling, lighting, fiber optic
communication systems, wireless and mobile telephony applications, optical and
electronic storage devices, computing, as well as a range of other leading-edge
technologies.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company markets and sells its products worldwide,
principally through its direct sales organization and appointed dealers and
sales representatives.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON&#146;s business activities include developing,
producing and installing equipment for coating semiconductor materials, process
engineering, consulting and training, including ongoing customer support.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON supplies to customers both full
production-scale complex material deposition systems and small scale systems
for Research and Development (R&amp;D) use and small-scale production use.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON&#146;s product range includes customized production
and research scale compound semiconductor systems capable of depositing
material films on up to 95 two-inch diameter wafers per single production run,
or smaller multiples of 4 to 6 inch diameter wafers, employing Metal-Organic
Chemical Vapor Deposition (MOCVD) or Hydride Vapor Phase Epitaxy (HVPE) or
organic thin film deposition on up to Gen. 3.5 substrates, including Polymer
Vapor Phase Deposition (PVPD) or Organic Vapor Phase Deposition (OVPD</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">) or large area deposition for Organic Light Emitting Diodes (OLED)
applications or Plasma Enhanced Chemical Vapor Phase Deposition (PECVD) for
depositing complex Carbon Nanostructures (Carbon Nanotubes or Nanowires).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON also manufactures full production and research
scale deposition systems for silicon semiconductor applications capable of
depositing material films on wafers of up to 300 mm diameter, employing
technologies such as: Chemical Vapor Deposition (CVD), Atomic Vapor Deposition
(AVD</font><font size="1" style="font-size:6.5pt;position:relative;top:-3.0pt;">&#174;</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">) and Atomic Layer Deposition (ALD).</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3<a name="PB_3_103946_3020"></a></font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">2.
Important Factors of the Reporting Period</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">US Dollar/Euro currency
development</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The US Dollar had started the year 2010 with an exchange rate of 1.43 USD
against the Euro and by the end of the first half year, had strengthened to
1.23 USD/EUR. By September&nbsp;30, 2010, the USD/EUR exchange rate had dropped
to 1.36 USD/EUR, with the European currency picking up against the US Dollar
during the third quarter of 2010. This development in the third quarter took
place against a backdrop of more positive European economic and reporting data,
combined with an improving opinion on the viability of Greek and other Euro
zone countries&#146; government savings and financing plans. It was also influenced
by the possibility, seen by some market observers, of further quantitative
monetary easing measures by the US Federal Reserve with a consequent weakening on
the US currency.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Over the whole reporting period, January&nbsp;1 until September&nbsp;30,
the US Dollar has nevertheless strengthened by 5%. The USD/EUR average exchange
rate, AIXTRON used for the income and expenses of this period, was 1.40 USD/EUR
in the first quarter, 1.31 USD/EUR in the second quarter, and 1.27 USD/EUR in
the third quarter of 2010. With the vast majority of AIXTRON&#146;s sales being
transacted in US Dollars, the net strengthening of the US Dollar within those
nine months has had a positive influence on AIXTRON&#146;s 9M/2010 revenues
translated into Euros. Since only a small portion of costs are occurred in US
Dollars, profitability also benefitted from the strengthening US Dollar,
despite some offsetting effects on operating margin from currency hedging and
translation expenses. For the remainder of the year, most of the anticipated
2010 cash flows have been hedged at an exchange rate of below 1.40 USD/EUR.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Sustained revenue growth with
healthy profitability leverage</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Supported by ongoing high system demand, mainly fuelled by HB LED
backlighting and lighting applications, and positively influenced by the
stronger US Dollar, Q3/2010 revenues further increased by 11% over the second
quarter to EUR 212.7m leading to cumulated 9M/2010 revenues of EUR 559.1m.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">While the quarterly gross profit increased only slightly by 4% to EUR
110.6m in Q3/2010 (with a 3 percentage points lower gross margin of 52%), the
operating result was significantly increased sequentially by 36% to EUR 82.6m
in Q3/2010 resulting in a 7 percentage points higher EBIT margin of 39%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Q3/2010 was the sixth sequential quarter of rising revenues and the fifth
sequential quarter of rising EBIT performance, underlining the positive
development of the AIXTRON business.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Also in terms of order intake, Q3/2010 represented the sixth sequential
growth quarter and, in line with Management expectations, 2010 equipment orders
continued to be recorded on a very high level (Q1/2010 EUR 168.5m; Q2/2010 EUR
175.4m; Q3/2010 EUR 200.4m).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">More than 30% of the LED system orders recorded in Q3/2010 were for AIXTRON&#146;s
latest generation systems that were launched in the first quarter of this year</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Tangible momentum in the
development of LED Lighting applications</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The LED lighting industry is seemingly gaining momentum, evidenced by an
increasing number of LED lighting fixtures being employed (for commercial,
industrial and municipal applications) and an increasing number of LED
replacement products for incandescent or fluorescent light bulbs becoming
available in retail outlets.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Government and public body regulatory requirements and financial incentive
and support programs are also being sustained in many international markets,
but particularly in Asia, encouraging and creating a healthy capital equipment
investment environment in the emerging LED lighting industry.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In September&nbsp;2010, AIXTRON announced a multiple order from the China
based Neo-Neon International Ltd., a company specializing in LED based light
replacement products. This specific order is a good regional example for the
increasing investment activity from companies targeting the LED general
lighting market. AIXTRON, as a leading player in the MOCVD equipment market,
expects to play a prominent role in this upcoming investment cycle.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the first nine months of 2010, several leading companies including Osram
Sylvania, Philips, GE, Cree, Toshiba, Panasonic and Samsung have launched or
announced general purpose LED lights designed to replace incandescent, halogen,
or compact fluorescent light sources. Most of the </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4<a name="PB_4_104016_7748"></a></font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">recent products being
offered online or in hardware stores, produce the equivalent light output of a
40-watt or 60-watt incandescent bulb. In addition to consuming far less
electricity than incandescent light bulbs, LED bulbs are also expected to last
for 20 years or more, they do not contain harmful mercury and have many other
advantages compared with incumbent technologies.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Whilst early product positioning prices of around USD 40 for a 60-watt
equivalent replacement product do not yet constitute the volume tipping point,
the recent ability and willingness of suppliers to drive this price down is
encouraging. The attractiveness of even premium priced products is increasingly
being driven by a greater consumer awareness of the lifetime costs of lighting.
The continuing momentum in this area, evident for the first time during this
reporting period, is very encouraging.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Significant progress with new
generation product acceptance</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">With further new generation MOCVD system orders received during Q3
especially from notable Chinese and Taiwanese customers (e.g. Sanan
Optoelectronics Co. Ltd., Neo-Neon International Ltd., Epistar, Tekcore), the
market acceptance of the recently launched next generation MOCVD systems is
progressing positively and in line with Management&#146;s expectations. More than
30% of the LED production system orders in the third quarter of 2010 were for
new generation systems; G5 and CRIUS II.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The new systems have the potential to</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> more
than double AIXTRON&#146;s customers&#146; productivity compared to the previous MOCVD
system generation. If customers opt for fully automated, clustered systems,
they could potentially achieve further substantial cost of ownership improvements.
</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We believe that these high volume production
systems are becoming increasingly attractive for customers planning and
preparing for the early adoption of LED lighting applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Research project &#147;EEMI450&#148; aiming
at 450mm silicon wafer equipment approved</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In Q3/2010, the EEMI450 joint research project, (European Equipment&nbsp;&amp;
Materials Initiative for 450 mm silicon wafers) funded by the EU and the German
government, was formally approved and started. The project is based upon a European
industrial initiative by equipment and material suppliers eager to become
engaged and competitive in 450mm wafer size technologies (i.e. wafer
manufacturing and characterization, metrology, wafer handling, automation, and
development of process modules, including the supply chain). Through a
coordinated approach, the EEMI450 partners expect to achieve considerable cost
of ownership savings, develop more competitive leading edge technology and
consequently; shorten the development cycle for a commercially and technically
viable 450mm product portfolio of equipment and processes.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The main task of AIXTRON will be to lead the efforts for the design,
development and building of a 450 mm showerhead deposition chamber for
multi-component materials. This will include the simulation, engineering and
manufacturing of critical equipment components.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt 14.2pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-14.2pt;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON is fully aware of the increasing market opportunities in the area
of Silicon based micro technology and expects to directly benefit from this
project by further strengthening the company&#146;s competitive positioning.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5<a name="PB_5_104039_141"></a></font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3. Results
of Operations</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3.1.
Development of Revenues</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the first nine months of 2010, AIXTRON recorded
revenues of EUR&nbsp;559.1m, an increase of EUR&nbsp;374.2m, or 202%, compared
to EUR&nbsp;184.9m in the same period last year. In addition to the significant
absolute sales volume effect, the revenue development in 9M/2010 was also
favorably influenced by the strengthening of the US Dollar during the first
nine months of 2010. In a year on year comparison, the period average internal
USD/EUR booking rate was approximately 4% stronger, therefore beneficial in
9M/2010, at 1.32 USD/EUR (average exchange rate 9M/2009: 1.37 USD/EUR).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The year on year increase in revenues was principally
due to the increase from Semiconductor deposition equipment revenues (9M/2010:
EUR 523.7m; 9M/2009: EUR 167.5m). The equipment bought by customers is
predominantly used for the production of LEDs, which in turn are primarily
employed as backlighting devices in products such as TVs, monitors, laptops,
netbooks, tablet PCs and emerging LED lighting applications. Total equipment
sales generated 94% of total revenues in 9M/2010 (91% in 9M/2009).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The remaining revenues were generated by sales of
spare parts and service which more than doubled compared to 9M/2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

  </td>
  <td width="2%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:2.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="10%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:10.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">103</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A very high percentage, namely 93%, of total revenues
in 9M/2010, were generated by sales to customers in Asia which is 13 percentage
points higher than the 80% recorded in 9M/2009. 3% of revenues in 9M/2010 were
generated in Europe (9M/2009: 15%) and the remaining 4% in the USA (9M/2009:
5%).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">-237</font></p>
  </td>
  <td width="1%" valign="bottom" bgcolor="#CCEEFF" style="background:#CCEEFF;padding:0in 0in 0in 0in;width:1.0%;">
  <p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:1.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cost of sales</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> increased year on year, by 150%, from EUR&nbsp;105.7m in 9M/2009 to
EUR&nbsp;264.6m in 9M/2010, while cost of sales relative to revenues,
significantly improved by 10 percentage points to 47% from 57% in 9M/2009. This
year on year improvement was mainly due to the increasing sales volume effect
and a more favorable product mix.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">While revenues increased by 202% and cost of sales by
150%, the Company&#146;s <b>gross profit</b>
increased by 272% year on year to EUR&nbsp;294.5m in 9M/2010 (9M/2009: EUR&nbsp;79.2m),
resulting in a 10 percentage points higher <b>gross margin</b> of
53% from 43% in 9M/2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Operating costs</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> increased year on year by 109% to EUR 104.9m (9M/2009: EUR&nbsp;50.2m).
Operating costs relative to revenues were 19% in 9M/2010, 8 percentage points lower
than the 27% in 9M/2009. This development was influenced by the following
factors:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Selling expenses</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> increased year on year (but to a lesser extent than revenues), by 145% to
EUR&nbsp;39.9m (9M/2009: EUR&nbsp;16.3m), mainly against a backdrop of higher
warranty expenses as a consequence of higher volume and sales commissions,
which vary by territory, partially offset by disproportionally lower increases
in discretionary expenses. Selling costs relative to revenues decreased year on
year by 2 percentage points to 7%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The year on year 35% increase in<b> general and
administration expenses</b> to EUR&nbsp;21.8m in 9M/2010 (9M/2009:
EUR&nbsp;16.1m) was principally due to profit-related variable administration
expenses, investments in infrastructure and consultancy expenses. General and
administration expenses, relative to revenues, significantly decreased from 9%
in 9M/2009 to only 4% in 9M/2010, principally due to the higher sales volume
effect.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Research and development costs</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> also increased by 35% year on year from EUR 24.9m recorded in 9M/2009 to
EUR&nbsp;33.5m in 9M/2010, due to the increase in development activities,
including additional personnel, material and equipment expenses. R&amp;D costs
decreased in relative terms from 13% of revenues in 9M/2009 to 6% in 9M/2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">However, AIXTRON&#146;s R&amp;D investment activities are
expected to remain very strong in the years to come, especially with the
increased development focus on the R&amp;D center being built at the Company&#146;s
Herzogenrath/Aachen County premises. The partial completion of Phase I of this
project will enable the planned relocation of engineering staff to commence
during November. In support of the increased focus on R&amp;D, the group has
completed a reorganization of its intellectual property to enable more
efficient use of resources throughout the group.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">These accelerated R&amp;D investments will support the
Company&#146;s determination to remain a major player in markets judged by many to
hold significant growth opportunities for many years to come.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Net <b>other operating income and
expenses</b> in the first nine months of 2010 resulted in an expense of </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7<a name="PB_7_105145_8146"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='7',FILE='C:\JMS\106202\10-19886-1\task4325965\19886-1-bc-01.htm',USER='106202',CD='Oct 27 23:17 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">EUR&nbsp;9.7m, compared with EUR&nbsp;7.1m of income
in 9M/2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Included in the other operating income recorded in
9M/2009 were some one-off effects from the sale of the Aachen office building
and compensation payments for cancelled orders, principally, in the first
quarter of 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In 9M/2010, a currency expense of EUR&nbsp;13.0m was
incurred largely from EUR/USD hedging contracts. Expenses of EUR 14.8m relate
to hedge contracts maturing during 9M/2010. This currency expense was partly
offset by positive effects from hedges for future cash flows and translation
gains of EUR 6.7m mainly from the balance sheet revaluation of advance payments
from customers. Other effects include transactional and translation
differences, which do not involve hedge contracts. EUR 2.5m of R&amp;D grants,
received in 9M/2010, were recorded as other operating income.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For the remaining 3 month period of the fiscal year,
AIXTRON has hedged the majority of anticipated 2010 cash flows at an exchange
rate below 1.40 USD/EUR.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The <b>operating result</b>
significantly increased by 554%, from EUR 29.0m in 9M/2009 to EUR 189.6m in
9M/2010 with an 18 percentage points higher EBIT margin of 34%. This
development was principally due to the positive effects of the increase in
revenue and the relatively lower costs as described above. At the same time,
the expense from currency hedges and currency translation effects offset, to a
limited extent, some of the positive effects on the operating result and
margin.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Result before taxes </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">increased by 543% from EUR 29.6m in 9M/2009 to EUR 190.3m in 9M/2010, with
a net finance income of EUR 0.7m in 9M/2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON recorded a <b>tax expense</b>
of EUR 59.4m in the first nine months of 2010, at a stable effective tax rate
of 31% (9M/2009: EUR 9.2m or 31% of the profit before taxes).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Net income</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> was 542% up year on year from EUR 20.4m (11% of revenues) in 9M/2009 to
EUR 130.9m (23% of revenues) in 9M/2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3.3.
Development of Orders</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As with revenue development; <b>equipment
order intake</b> significantly increased in the first nine months of
2010. 9M/2010 order intake was 163% up year on year, at EUR 544.3m (9M/2009:
EUR 206.7m). Q3/2010 order intake was recorded 14% above the prior quarter,
sustaining the already high level of demand achieved in the prior sequential
quarters (Q1/2010: EUR 168.5m; Q2/2010: 175.4m; Q3/2010: 200.4m). As a result;
Q3/2010 is now the sixth sequential quarter in terms of rising order intake
(and revenues).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As a matter of internal policy, order intake in US
Dollars is recorded at the current budget exchange rate, which for 2010, had
been previously set at USD 1.50/EUR.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The continuing positive market development for
compound semiconductor equipment reflects the increased adoption of LED
backlighting in TV and other display applications, representing what the
industry has called the &#145;Second LED Investment Cycle&#146;.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Included in more recent order intake however, is a
number of orders linked to LED-lighting applications, which underline a growing
momentum for the emergence of an LED lighting market and the earlier than
anticipated development of what is being described by some observers as the &#145;Third
Investment Cycle&#146; for the LED industry.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">It is still not yet explicitly clear how imminent or
meaningful that investment cycle is at this particular point in time or how far
away the &#145;key volume tipping point&#146; is. However, the AIXTRON Executive Board
opinion is that current developments in the LED industry could potentially pull
forward the emergence of a sustainable LED Lighting market in volume terms.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8<a name="PB_8_105345_7091"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company&#146;s intention is to have developed the next
generation AIXTRON system technology within the next two to three years,
reflecting the Company&#146;s positive assumptions on the emergence of a meaningful
and sustainable LED Lighting market.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The total <b>equipment order backlog</b>
of EUR 278.7m at September&nbsp;30, 2010 was 83% higher than at the same point
in time in 2009 (September&nbsp;30, 2009: EUR 152.4m).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As a matter of internal policy, AIXTRON records only
systems as order intake and order backlog, if the Company has received a firm
purchase order, an agreed deposit, any specific shipment dependant
documentation, and a system specific customer confirmed delivery date.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Also as a matter of internal policy, US Dollar
denominated order backlog is recorded at the current budget exchange rate,
which for 2010, had been previously set at USD1.50/EUR.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9<a name="PB_9_105400_455"></a></font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><hr size="3" width="100%" noshade color="#010101" align="left"></div>

<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='9',FILE='C:\JMS\106202\10-19886-1\task4325965\19886-1-bc-01.htm',USER='106202',CD='Oct 27 23:17 2010' -->


<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">4. Financial Position and Net Assets</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company recorded no <b>bank borrowings</b> as of September&nbsp;30,
2010 and December&nbsp;31, 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The <b>equity ratio</b>
decreased to 66% as of September&nbsp;30,&nbsp;2010, from 72% as of December&nbsp;31,&nbsp;2009,
principally due to higher asset levels and a consequently higher balance sheet
total.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The AIXTRON Group&#146;s <b>capital
expenditures</b> of the first nine months of 2010 amounted to EUR 19.1m
(9M/2009: EUR 6.8m), the large majority of which was related to investments
into the new R&amp;D center and purchases of technical equipment, including
testing and laboratory equipment.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Cash and cash equivalents </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(including cash deposits with a maturity of more than three months, most of
which is held in Euros), increased by 48% to EUR 444.6m (EUR 262.6m + EUR
182.0m cash deposits) as of September&nbsp;30,&nbsp;2010 compared to EUR 301.2m
(EUR 211.2m + EUR 90.0m cash deposits) as of December&nbsp;31, 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The value of <b>property, plant and equipment</b> increased by
31% to EUR&nbsp;49.6m as per September&nbsp;30, 2010 (EUR 37.8m as of December&nbsp;31,
2009), principally due to an increase in laboratory equipment (with
depreciation partly offsetting investments in technical equipment) and the
initial investments for the new R&amp;D center.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The increase in the value of <b>goodwill </b>from
EUR 58.3m as per December&nbsp;31, 2009 to
EUR 60.8m as per September&nbsp;30,
2010 resulted purely from currency translation adjustments. There were no
additions or impairments in the first nine months of 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The value of <b>other intangible assets</b>
remained stable at EUR 7.8m as per December&nbsp;31, 2009 and September&nbsp;30, 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Inventories,</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> including raw materials, work in progress and finished goods, increased by
71% from EUR 89.6m as of December&nbsp;31,
2009 to EUR 153.2m as of September&nbsp;30, 2010, in line with higher manufacturing volumes.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Trade receivables</font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> also increased by 30% from EUR 49.3m as of December&nbsp;31, 2009 to EUR
63.9m as of September&nbsp;30, 2010, due
directly to the increased business volume.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10<a name="PB_10_105420_4141"></a></font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">5.
Opportunities and Risks</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON believes that the following market trends and <b>opportunities</b> in the relevant end user markets could have a
positive effect on future business:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Short Term</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Continuing
investment into capacity expansion for the production of LED backlighting for
LCD screens (netbooks, tablets, laptops, monitors, TVs).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Further
increased adoption of LEDs in automotive (e.g. vehicle interior lighting,
headlights and rear lights) or other applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increased
adoption of LEDs for interior, exterior, public, street and professional
lighting.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Mid Term</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increased
adoption of LEDs for consumer and residential general lighting applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increased
emergence of high volume Silicon Carbide (SiC) production applications and
emerging hybrid automotive and photovoltaic transistor applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increased
emergence and further development of plastic electronics / flexible organic TFT
backplanes.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Development
of next generation NAND, DRAM and PRAM memory applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Increased
development activity for specialized compound solar cell applications.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Long Term</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Further
progress in research activities leading to technologies for OLED lighting and
displays as well as organic material large area deposition.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Progress
in the convergence development of new complex semiconductor material
applications as substituting materials in the silicon semiconductor industry.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Symbol" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#183;</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Development
of new applications using Carbon Nanostructures (Carbon Nanotubes or Carbon
Nanowires).</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON is exposed to a series of <b>risks</b>
which are described in detail in the &#147;Risk Report&#148; of the Annual Report 2009
and in the section &#147;Risk Factors&#148; in AIXTRON&#146;s 2009 20-F-Report, which has been
filed with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission on March&nbsp;10, 2010.
Copies of the Company&#146;s most recent Annual Report and Form&nbsp;20-F are
available on the Company&#146;s website at www.aixtron.com (sections &#147;Investors/Reports&#148;
and &#147;Investors/US-Listing&#148;), as well as on the SEC&#146;s website at www.sec.gov.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">International Rectifier Corporation (I.R.), of El
Segundo, California, USA filed a complaint on September&nbsp;8, 2008 in the
U.S. District Court for the Central District of California against seven of
I.R.&#146;s former employees, including I.R.&#146;s founder and former CEO Alex Lidow, as
well as five companies, including AIXTRON AG. I.R.&#146;s complaint alleged that
I.R.&#146;s seven former employees misappropriated, divulged to a business named
Efficient Power conversion Corporation (EPCC) and illegally used trade secrets
of I.R. relating to Gallium Nitride Technology (GaN). I.R. also alleged that
some of the companies, including AIXTRON aided the seven main defendants by
providing additional information relevant to the technology at issue. In February&nbsp;2009,
the U.S. District Court dismissed the two U.S. federal claims in the case
against the defendants and declined to exercise its discretionary jurisdiction
over the remaining claims, which all arose under California law. Having had its
lawsuit dismissed in the U.S. District Court,&nbsp;I.R. re-filed essentially
the same lawsuit in California state court in March&nbsp;2009 based on the
California state claims alone, and alleged five causes of action against
AIXTRON. After multiple rounds of motions to dismiss,&nbsp;I.R. dropped some of
its claims against the defendants, and the California court dismissed
additional claims. Two of I.R.&#146;s claims, one for alleged misappropriation of
trade secrets and one for alleged breach of contract, remain in the case
against AIXTRON AG. The lawsuit seeks USD 61m in damages jointly and severally
against all of the defendants, plus exemplary damages and attorneys&#146; fees and
legal costs against AIXTRON AG, and punitive damages against other defendants.
AIXTRON AG fully rejects the allegations contained in I.R.&#146;s California lawsuit
and is vigorously defending itself against the two remaining claims raised in
I.R.&#146;s California action against AIXTRON AG. Furthermore, AIXTRON AG filed an
action in the Aachen Landgericht in Germany (case no. 41 O 121/08) for a
negative declaratory judgment against I.R. with the aim of establishing in
Germany, and in the U.S., that all allegations and claims that I.R. raised
against AIXTRON AG are unfounded (the &#147;German action&#148;). In the German action,&nbsp;I.R.
counterclaimed for injunctive relief and damages. On April&nbsp;7, 2009, the Aachen
Landgericht issued a judgment in favor of AIXTRON AG and against I.R. on all of
AIXTRON AG&#146;s claims and all of I.R.&#146;s counterclaims in the German action. The
time for I.R. to appeal against the judgment in the German action has expired,
and the judgment in favor </font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11<a name="PB_11_111045_8627"></a></font></p>

<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">of AIXTRON AG and against I.R. in the German action is
final and res judicata. AIXTRON AG reserves the right to seek recovery from
I.R. of any and all costs and damages that might result from I.R.&#146;s unjustified
allegations and the proceedings brought by I.R. against AIXTRON AG.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In times of substantial demand for MOCVD systems, LED
manufacturers may experience difficulties in maintaining a sufficient flow of
raw materials to achieve their increased manufacturing output. Should this
occur, customers could request delays to AIXTRON system shipments.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the first nine months of 2010, AIXTRON
Management was not aware of any further significant additions or changes in the
risks as described in the 2009 Annual Report/20-F-Report referred to above.</font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">6. Outlook</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">It is clear that 2010 will be another growth year with
record manufacturing output levels for AIXTRON. The very solid order backlog of
EUR 278.7m at the end of the nine months period represents an excellent
foundation for the Management&#146;s expectation of the revenue and profit
development in the remaining three months of 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We expect that about EUR 180m of the period end
backlog as per September&nbsp;30, 2010, will be converted into revenues by the
end of the year 2010. We expect to record a further EUR 11m of spares and
service revenue during 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Taking the above into account, and the current USD/EUR
exchange rate levels, the Executive Board continues to be confident of
achieving the 2010 full year revenue guidance of circa EUR 750m and has decided
to increase the EBIT margin guidance to circa 35%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Due
to multiple emerging market applications for LED products, we </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">also remain optimistic on the evident medium to
long term trend</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">. Both, market volume and
the penetration rate of LEDs as backlighting units in products such as
netbooks, tablets, laptops, monitors and TVs, are expected to continue to grow
in the short- to mid-term, and the adoption of LEDs for general lighting applications
is expected to increase.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We will continue to closely watch the USD/EUR exchange
rate and the potential effects on the Company&#146;s revenues and profitability and
will employ appropriate financial instruments to mitigate potential risk.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
Company is expecting to execute the shareholder approval to convert to an SE
(Socielas Europaea) at the end of the year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the remaining three months of the year, we plan
to continue to invest in laboratory equipment and to complete the roll out of
the group-wide SAP Enterprise Software System. Investment in the building of
the new R&amp;D center at our premises in Herzogenrath/Aachen County is
expected to reach about EUR 15m by the end of the year.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We continue to believe that our Company has sufficient
funds or instruments in place to ensure that the foreseeable needs of the
business can be met.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As at September&nbsp;30, 2010, we had no binding
agreements for participation financing, company acquisitions or transfers of
parts of the Company.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">13<a name="PB_13_111115_3736"></a></font></p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Interim
Financial Statements</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Additional
Disclosures</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">1. Accounting Policies</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">This consolidated interim financial report of AIXTRON
AG has been prepared in accordance with International Financial Reporting
Standards (IFRS) applicable for Interim Financial Reporting,&nbsp;IAS 34.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The accounting policies adopted in this interim
financial report are consistent with those followed in the preparation of the
Group&#146;s annual financial statements for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The consolidated interim financial statements of
AIXTRON AG include the following operating subsidiaries (collectively referred
to as &#147;AIXTRON&#148;, &#147;the AIXTRON Group&#148;, or &#147;the Company&#148;): AIXTRON,&nbsp;Inc.,
Sunnyvale (USA); AIXTRON Ltd., Cambridge (United Kingdom); AIXTRON AB, Lund
(Sweden); AIXTRON Korea Co. Ltd., Seoul (South Korea); AIXTRON KK, Tokyo
(Japan); and AIXTRON Taiwan Co. Ltd., Hsinchu (Taiwan). There were no changes
in the consolidated group of companies in comparison with December&nbsp;31,
2009.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">2. Segment Reporting</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following
segment information has been prepared in accordance with IFRS 8 &#147;Operating
Segments&#148;. As AIXTRON has only one operating segment, the information provided
relates only to geographical data.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The Company markets and sells its products in Asia,
Europe, and the United States, mainly through its direct sales organization and
cooperation partners.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In presenting information on the basis of geographical
segments, segment revenue is based on the geographical location of customers.
Segment assets are based on the geographical location of the assets.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3. Stock Option Plans</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">In the first nine months of 2010, AIXTRON&#146;s employees
and Executive Board members held stock options, representing the right to
receive AIXTRON AG common shares or AIXTRON AG American Depositary Shares
(ADS). The status of these options developed as follows:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">4.
Employees</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The total number of full time equivalent employees
rose from 649 on September&nbsp;30, 2009 to 766 persons on September&nbsp;30,
2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

changes to the composition of the Company&#146;s Executive and Supervisory Boards as
of September&nbsp;30, 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">AIXTRON did not conclude or carry out any material transactions
with related parties.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">7.
Post-Balance Sheet Date Events</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">There were no known business events with a potentially
significant effect on AIXTRON&#146;s results of operation, financial position or net
assets after September&nbsp;30, 2010.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Responsibility
Statement</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To the best of our
knowledge, and in accordance with the applicable reporting principles for
interim financial reporting, the interim consolidated financial statements for
the nine months ended September&nbsp;30, 2010 give a true and fair view of the
assets, liabilities, financial position and profit or loss of the group, and
the interim management report of the group includes a fair review of the
development and performance of the business and the position of the group,
together with a description of the principal </font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">opportunities
and risks associated with the expected development of the group for the
remaining months of the financial year.</font></p>
